The fields listed before the lock\n// should not be changed; the fields listed after the\n// lock must be accessed only while holding the lock.\n//\n// The methods of this type follow the naming convention that the\n// suffix \"Locked\" means the caller must hold the lock; for a method\n// whose name does not end in \"Locked\" either acquires the lock or\n// does not care about locking.\n//\n// The methods of this type also follow the convention that the suffix\n// \"ToBoundLocked\" means that the caller may have to follow up with a\n// call to `boundNextDispatchLocked`.  This is so for a method that\n// changes what request is oldest in a queue, because that change means\n// that the anti-windup hack in boundNextDispatchLocked needs to be\n// applied wrt the revised oldest request in the queue.\ntype queueSet struct {\n\tclock                    eventclock.Interface\n\testimatedServiceDuration time.Duration\n\n\treqsGaugePair metrics.RatioedGaugePair // .RequestsExecuting covers regular phase only\n\n\texecSeatsGauge metrics.RatioedGauge // for all phases of execution\n\n\tseatDemandIntegrator metrics.Gauge\n\n\tpromiseFactory promiseFactory\n\n\tlock sync.Mutex\n\n\t// qCfg holds the current queuing configuration.  Its\n\t// DesiredNumQueues may be less than the current number of queues.\n\t// If its DesiredNumQueues is zero then its other queuing\n\t// parameters retain the settings they had when DesiredNumQueues\n\t// was last non-zero (if ever).\n\tqCfg fq.QueuingConfig\n\n\t// the current dispatching configuration.\n\tdCfg fq.DispatchingConfig\n\n\t// If `qCfg.DesiredNumQueues` is non-zero then dealer is not nil\n\t// and is good for `qCfg`.\n\tdealer *shufflesharding.Dealer\n\n\t// queues may be longer than the desired number, while the excess\n\t// queues are still draining.\n\tqueues []*queue\n\n\t// currentR is the amount of seat-seconds allocated per queue since process startup.\n\t// This is our generalization of the progress meter named R in the original fair queuing work.\n\tcurrentR fqrequest.SeatSeconds\n\n\t// lastRealTime is what `clock.Now()` yielded when `virtualTime` was last updated\n\tlastRealTime time.Time\n\n\t// robinIndex is the index of the last queue dispatched\n\trobinIndex int\n\n\t// totRequestsWaiting is the sum, over all the queues, of the\n\t// number of requests waiting in that queue\n\ttotRequestsWaiting int\n\n\t// totRequestsExecuting is the total number of requests of this\n\t// queueSet that are currently executing.  That is the same as the\n\t// sum, over all the queues, of the number of requests executing\n\t// from that queue.\n\ttotRequestsExecuting int\n\n\t// requestsExecutingSet is the set of requests executing in the real world IF\n\t// there are no queues; otherwise the requests are tracked in the queues.\n\trequestsExecutingSet sets.Set[*request]\n\n\t// totSeatsInUse is the number of total \"seats\" in use by all the\n\t// request(s) that are currently executing in this queueset.\n\ttotSeatsInUse int\n\n\t// totSeatsWaiting is the sum, over all the waiting requests, of their\n\t// max width.\n\ttotSeatsWaiting int\n\n\t// enqueues is the number of requests that have ever been enqueued\n\tenqueues int\n\n\t// totRequestsDispatched is the total number of requests of this\n\t// queueSet that have been processed.\n\ttotRequestsDispatched int\n\n\t// totRequestsRejected is the total number of requests of this\n\t// queueSet that have been rejected.\n\ttotRequestsRejected int\n\n\t// totRequestsTimedout is the total number of requests of this\n\t// queueSet that have been timeouted.\n\ttotRequestsTimedout int\n\n\t// totRequestsCancelled is the total number of requests of this\n\t// queueSet that have been cancelled.\n\ttotRequestsCancelled int\n}\n\n// NewQueueSetFactory creates a new QueueSetFactory object\nfunc NewQueueSetFactory(c eventclock.Interface) fq.QueueSetFactory {\n\treturn newTestableQueueSetFactory(c, ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory)\n}\n\n// newTestableQueueSetFactory creates a new QueueSetFactory object with the given promiseFactoryFactory\nfunc newTestableQueueSetFactory(c eventclock.Interface, promiseFactoryFactory promiseFactoryFactory) fq.QueueSetFactory {\n\treturn &queueSetFactory{\n\t\tclock:                 c,\n\t\tpromiseFactoryFactory: promiseFactoryFactory,\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (qsf *queueSetFactory) BeginConstruction(qCfg fq.QueuingConfig, reqsGaugePair metrics.RatioedGaugePair, execSeatsGauge metrics.RatioedGauge, seatDemandIntegrator metrics.Gauge) (fq.QueueSetCompleter, error) {\n\tdealer, err := checkConfig(qCfg)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn &queueSetCompleter{\n\t\tfactory:              qsf,\n\t\treqsGaugePair:        reqsGaugePair,\n\t\texecSeatsGauge:       execSeatsGauge,\n\t\tseatDemandIntegrator: seatDemandIntegrator,\n\t\tqCfg:                 qCfg,\n\t\tdealer:               dealer}, nil\n}\n\n// checkConfig returns a non-nil Dealer if the config is valid and\n// calls for one, and returns a non-nil error if the given config is\n// invalid.\nfunc checkConfig(qCfg fq.QueuingConfig) (*shufflesharding.Dealer, error) {\n\tif qCfg.DesiredNumQueues <= 0 {\n\t\treturn nil, nil\n\t}\n\tdealer, err := shufflesharding.NewDealer(qCfg.DesiredNumQueues, qCfg.HandSize)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\terr = fmt.Errorf(\"the QueueSetConfig implies an invalid shuffle sharding config (DesiredNumQueues is deckSize): %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn dealer, err\n}\n\nfunc (qsc *queueSetCompleter) Complete(dCfg fq.DispatchingConfig) fq.QueueSet {\n\tqs := qsc.theSet\n\tif qs == nil {\n\t\tqs = &queueSet{\n\t\t\tclock:                    qsc.factory.clock,\n\t\t\testimatedServiceDuration: 3 * time.Millisecond,\n\t\t\treqsGaugePair:            qsc.reqsGaugePair,\n\t\t\texecSeatsGauge:           qsc.execSeatsGauge,\n\t\t\tseatDemandIntegrator:     qsc.seatDemandIntegrator,\n\t\t\tqCfg:                     qsc.qCfg,\n\t\t\tcurrentR:                 0,\n\t\t\tlastRealTime:             qsc.factory.clock.Now(),\n\t\t\trequestsExecutingSet:     sets.New[*request](),\n\t\t}\n\t\tqs.promiseFactory = qsc.factory.promiseFactoryFactory(qs)\n\t}\n\tqs.setConfiguration(context.Background(), qsc.qCfg, qsc.dealer, dCfg)\n\treturn qs\n}\n\n// createQueues is a helper method for initializing an array of n queues\nfunc createQueues(n, baseIndex int) []*queue {\n\tfqqueues := make([]*queue, n)\n\tfor i := 0; i < n; i++ {\n\t\tfqqueues[i] = &queue{index: baseIndex + i, requestsWaiting: newRequestFIFO(), requestsExecuting: sets.New[*request]()}\n\t}\n\treturn fqqueues\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) BeginConfigChange(qCfg fq.QueuingConfig) (fq.QueueSetCompleter, error) {\n\tdealer, err := checkConfig(qCfg)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\treturn &queueSetCompleter{\n\t\ttheSet: qs,\n\t\tqCfg:   qCfg,\n\t\tdealer: dealer}, nil\n}\n\n// setConfiguration is used to set the configuration for a queueSet.\n// Update handling for when fields are updated is handled here as well -\n// eg: if DesiredNum is increased, setConfiguration reconciles by\n// adding more queues.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) setConfiguration(ctx context.Context, qCfg fq.QueuingConfig, dealer *shufflesharding.Dealer, dCfg fq.DispatchingConfig) {\n\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\n\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n\n\tif qCfg.DesiredNumQueues > 0 {\n\t\t// Adding queues is the only thing that requires immediate action\n\t\t// Removing queues is handled by attrition, removing a queue when\n\t\t// it goes empty and there are too many.\n\t\tnumQueues := len(qs.queues)\n\t\tif qCfg.DesiredNumQueues > numQueues {\n\t\t\tqs.queues = append(qs.queues,\n\t\t\t\tcreateQueues(qCfg.DesiredNumQueues-numQueues, len(qs.queues))...)\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tqCfg.QueueLengthLimit = qs.qCfg.QueueLengthLimit\n\t\tqCfg.HandSize = qs.qCfg.HandSize\n\t}\n\n\tqs.qCfg = qCfg\n\tqs.dCfg = dCfg\n\tqs.dealer = dealer\n\tqll := qCfg.QueueLengthLimit\n\tif qll < 1 {\n\t\tqll = 1\n\t}\n\tif qCfg.DesiredNumQueues > 0 {\n\t\tqll *= qCfg.DesiredNumQueues\n\t}\n\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.SetDenominator(float64(qll))\n\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.SetDenominator(float64(dCfg.ConcurrencyDenominator))\n\tqs.execSeatsGauge.SetDenominator(float64(dCfg.ConcurrencyDenominator))\n\n\tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n}\n\n// A decision about a request\ntype requestDecision int\n\n// Values passed through a request's decision\nconst (\n\t// Serve this one\n\tdecisionExecute requestDecision = iota\n\n\t// This one's context timed out / was canceled\n\tdecisionCancel\n)\n\n// StartRequest begins the process of handling a request.  We take the\n// approach of updating the metrics about total requests queued and\n// executing at each point where there is a change in that quantity,\n// because the metrics --- and only the metrics --- track that\n// quantity per FlowSchema.\n// The queueSet's promiseFactory is invoked once if the returned Request is non-nil,\n// not invoked if the Request is nil.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) StartRequest(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) (fq.Request, bool) {\n\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\n\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n\tvar req *request\n\n\t// ========================================================================\n\t// Step 0:\n\t// Apply only concurrency limit, if zero queues desired\n\tif qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 1 {\n\t\tif !qs.canAccommodateSeatsLocked(workEstimate.MaxSeats()) {\n\t\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v because %d seats are asked for, %d seats are in use (%d are executing) and the limit is %d\",\n\t\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2, workEstimate, qs.totSeatsInUse, qs.totRequestsExecuting, qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)\n\t\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n\t\t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"concurrency-limit\")\n\t\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n\t\t}\n\t\treq = qs.dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n\t\treturn req, false\n\t}\n\n\t// ========================================================================\n\t// Step 1:\n\t// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n\t// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n\t// we are at max queue length\n\t// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n\treq = qs.shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, hashValue, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2, queueNoteFn)\n\t// req == nil means that the request was rejected - no remaining\n\t// concurrency shares and at max queue length already\n\tif req == nil {\n\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v due to queue full\", qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n\t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"queue-full\")\n\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n\t}\n\n\t// ========================================================================\n\t// Step 2:\n\t// The next step is to invoke the method that dequeues as much\n\t// as possible.\n\t// This method runs a loop, as long as there are non-empty\n\t// queues and the number currently executing is less than the\n\t// assured concurrency value.  The body of the loop uses the\n\t// fair queuing technique to pick a queue and dispatch a\n\t// request from that queue.\n\tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n\n\treturn req, false\n}\n\n// ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory is the promiseFactoryFactory that\n// a queueSetFactory would ordinarily use.\n// Test code might use something different.\nfunc ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory(qs *queueSet) promiseFactory {\n\treturn promise.NewWriteOnce\n}\n\n// MaxSeats returns the maximum number of seats this request requires, it is\n// the maxumum of the two - WorkEstimate.InitialSeats, WorkEstimate.FinalSeats.\nfunc (req *request) MaxSeats() int {\n\treturn req.workEstimate.MaxSeats()\n}\n\nfunc (req *request) InitialSeats() int {\n\treturn int(req.workEstimate.InitialSeats)\n}\n\nfunc (req *request) NoteQueued(inQueue bool) {\n\tif req.queueNoteFn != nil {\n\t\treq.queueNoteFn(inQueue)\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (req *request) Finish(execFn func()) bool {\n\texec, idle := req.wait()\n\tif !exec {\n\t\treturn idle\n\t}\n\tfunc() {\n\t\tdefer func() {\n\t\t\tidle = req.qs.finishRequestAndDispatchAsMuchAsPossible(req)\n\t\t}()\n\n\t\texecFn()\n\t}()\n\n\treturn idle\n}\n\nfunc (req *request) wait() (bool, bool) {\n\tqs := req.qs\n\n\t// ========================================================================\n\t// Step 3:\n\t// The final step is to wait on a decision from\n\t// somewhere and then act on it.\n\tdecisionAny := req.decision.Get()\n\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(req.ctx)\n\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n\tif req.waitStarted {\n\t\t// This can not happen, because the client is forbidden to\n\t\t// call Wait twice on the same request\n\t\tklog.Errorf(\"Duplicate call to the Wait method!  Immediately returning execute=false.  QueueSet=%s, startTime=%s, descr1=%#+v, descr2=%#+v\", req.qs.qCfg.Name, req.startTime, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n\t\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n\t}\n\treq.waitStarted = true\n\tswitch decisionAny {\n\tcase decisionCancel: // handle in code following this switch\n\tcase decisionExecute:\n\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Dispatching request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n\t\treturn true, false\n\tdefault:\n\t\t// This can not happen, all possible values are handled above\n\t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s): Impossible decision (type %T, value %#+v) for request %#+v %#+v!  Treating as cancel\", qs.qCfg.Name, decisionAny, decisionAny, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n\t}\n\t// TODO(aaron-prindle) add metrics for this case\n\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Ejecting request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n\t// remove the request from the queue as its queue wait time has exceeded\n\tqueue := req.queue\n\tif req.removeFromQueueLocked() != nil {\n\t\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n\t\tqs.totRequestsWaiting--\n\t\tqs.totSeatsWaiting -= req.MaxSeats()\n\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n\t\tqs.totRequestsCancelled++\n\t\tmetrics.AddReject(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, \"time-out\")\n\t\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -1)\n\t\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -req.MaxSeats())\n\t\treq.NoteQueued(false)\n\t\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(-1)\n\t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n\t}\n\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) IsIdle() bool {\n\tqs.lock.Lock()\n\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n\treturn qs.isIdleLocked()\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) isIdleLocked() bool {\n\treturn qs.totRequestsWaiting == 0 && qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0\n}\n\n// lockAndSyncTime acquires the lock and updates the virtual time.\n// Doing them together avoids the mistake of modifying some queue state\n// before calling syncTimeLocked.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) lockAndSyncTime(ctx context.Context) {\n\tqs.lock.Lock()\n\tqs.syncTimeLocked(ctx)\n}\n\n// syncTimeLocked updates the virtual time based on the assumption\n// that the current state of the queues has been in effect since\n// `qs.lastRealTime`.  Thus, it should be invoked after acquiring the\n// lock and before modifying the state of any queue.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) syncTimeLocked(ctx context.Context) {\n\trealNow := qs.clock.Now()\n\ttimeSinceLast := realNow.Sub(qs.lastRealTime)\n\tqs.lastRealTime = realNow\n\tprevR := qs.currentR\n\tincrR := fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(qs.getVirtualTimeRatioLocked(), timeSinceLast)\n\tqs.currentR = prevR + incrR\n\tswitch {\n\tcase prevR > qs.currentR:\n\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queueset::currentR overflow\"), \"Overflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", realNow.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"prevR\", prevR, \"incrR\", incrR, \"currentR\", qs.currentR)\n\tcase qs.currentR >= highR:\n\t\tqs.advanceEpoch(ctx, realNow, incrR)\n\t}\n\tmetrics.SetCurrentR(qs.qCfg.Name, qs.currentR.ToFloat())\n}\n\n// rDecrement is the amount by which the progress meter R is wound backwards\n// when needed to avoid overflow.\nconst rDecrement = fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds / 2\n\n// highR is the threshold that triggers advance of the epoch.\n// That is, decrementing the global progress meter R by rDecrement.\nconst highR = rDecrement + rDecrement/2\n\n// advanceEpoch subtracts rDecrement from the global progress meter R\n// and all the readings that have been taked from that meter.\n// The now and incrR parameters are only used to add info to the log messages.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) advanceEpoch(ctx context.Context, now time.Time, incrR fqrequest.SeatSeconds) {\n\toldR := qs.currentR\n\tqs.currentR -= rDecrement\n\tklog.InfoS(\"Advancing epoch\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", now.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"oldR\", oldR, \"newR\", qs.currentR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n\tsuccess := true\n\tfor qIdx, queue := range qs.queues {\n\t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 {\n\t\t\t// Do not just decrement, the value could be quite outdated.\n\t\t\t// It is safe to reset to zero in this case, because the next request\n\t\t\t// will overwrite the zero with `qs.currentR`.\n\t\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = 0\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\toldNextDispatchR := queue.nextDispatchR\n\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR -= rDecrement\n\t\tif queue.nextDispatchR > oldNextDispatchR {\n\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queue::nextDispatchR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"oldNextDispatchR\", oldNextDispatchR, \"newNextDispatchR\", queue.nextDispatchR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n\t\t\tsuccess = false\n\t\t}\n\t\tqueue.requestsWaiting.Walk(func(req *request) bool {\n\t\t\toldArrivalR := req.arrivalR\n\t\t\treq.arrivalR -= rDecrement\n\t\t\tif req.arrivalR > oldArrivalR {\n\t\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"request::arrivalR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"request\", *req, \"oldArrivalR\", oldArrivalR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n\t\t\t\tsuccess = false\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\tmetrics.AddEpochAdvance(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, success)\n}\n\n// getVirtualTimeRatio calculates the rate at which virtual time has\n// been advancing, according to the logic in `doc.go`.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) getVirtualTimeRatioLocked() float64 {\n\tactiveQueues := 0\n\tseatsRequested := 0\n\tfor _, queue := range qs.queues {\n\t\t// here we want the sum of the maximum width of the requests in this queue since our\n\t\t// goal is to find the maximum rate at which the queue could work.\n\t\tseatsRequested += (queue.seatsInUse + queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum().MaxSeatsSum)\n\t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() > 0 || queue.requestsExecuting.Len() > 0 {\n\t\t\tactiveQueues++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif activeQueues == 0 {\n\t\treturn 0\n\t}\n\treturn math.Min(float64(seatsRequested), float64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)) / float64(activeQueues)\n}\n\n// shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked encapsulates the logic required\n// to validate and enqueue a request for the queueSet/QueueSet:\n// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n// we are at max queue length\n// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n// returns the enqueud request on a successful enqueue\n// returns nil in the case that there is no available concurrency or\n// the queuelengthlimit has been reached\nfunc (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) *request {\n\t// Start with the shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n\tqueueIdx := qs.shuffleShardLocked(hashValue, descr1, descr2)\n\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n\n\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n\n\t// Create a request and enqueue\n\treq := &request{\n\t\tqs:                qs,\n\t\tfsName:            fsName,\n\t\tflowDistinguisher: flowDistinguisher,\n\t\tctx:               ctx,\n\t\tdecision:          qs.promiseFactory(nil, ctx, decisionCancel),\n\t\tarrivalTime:       qs.clock.Now(),\n\t\tarrivalR:          qs.currentR,\n\t\tqueue:             queue,\n\t\tdescr1:            descr1,\n\t\tdescr2:            descr2,\n\t\tqueueNoteFn:       queueNoteFn,\n\t\tworkEstimate:      qs.completeWorkEstimate(workEstimate),\n\t}\n\tif ok := qs.rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(req); !ok {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\tmetrics.ObserveQueueLength(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, queue.requestsWaiting.Length())\n\treturn req\n}\n\n// shuffleShardLocked uses shuffle sharding to select a queue index\n// using the given hashValue and the shuffle sharding parameters of the queueSet.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardLocked(hashValue uint64, descr1, descr2 interface{}) int {\n\tvar backHand [8]int\n\t// Deal into a data structure, so that the order of visit below is not necessarily the order of the deal.\n\t// This removes bias in the case of flows with overlapping hands.\n\thand := qs.dealer.DealIntoHand(hashValue, backHand[:])\n\thandSize := len(hand)\n\toffset := qs.enqueues % handSize\n\tqs.enqueues++\n\tbestQueueIdx := -1\n\tminQueueSeatSeconds := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n\tfor i := 0; i < handSize; i++ {\n\t\tqueueIdx := hand[(offset+i)%handSize]\n\t\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n\t\tqueueSum := queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum()\n\n\t\t// this is the total amount of work in seat-seconds for requests\n\t\t// waiting in this queue, we will select the queue with the minimum.\n\t\tthisQueueSeatSeconds := queueSum.TotalWorkSum\n\t\tklog.V(7).Infof(\"QS(%s): For request %#+v %#+v considering queue %d with sum: %#v and %d seats in use, nextDispatchR=%v\", qs.qCfg.Name, descr1, descr2, queueIdx, queueSum, queue.seatsInUse, queue.nextDispatchR)\n\t\tif thisQueueSeatSeconds < minQueueSeatSeconds {\n\t\t\tminQueueSeatSeconds = thisQueueSeatSeconds\n\t\t\tbestQueueIdx = queueIdx\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\tif klogV := klog.V(6); klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\tchosenQueue := qs.queues[bestQueueIdx]\n\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: For request %#+v %#+v chose queue %d, with sum: %#v & %d seats in use & nextDispatchR=%v\", qs.qCfg.Name, qs.clock.Now().Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, descr1, descr2, bestQueueIdx, chosenQueue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum(), chosenQueue.seatsInUse, chosenQueue.nextDispatchR)\n\t}\n\treturn bestQueueIdx\n}\n\n// rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked rejects or enqueues the newly arrived\n// request, which has been assigned to a queue.  If up against the\n// queue length limit and the concurrency limit then returns false.\n// Otherwise enqueues and returns true.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) bool {\n\tqueue := request.queue\n\tcurQueueLength := queue.requestsWaiting.Length()\n\t// rejects the newly arrived request if resource criteria not met\n\tif qs.totSeatsInUse >= qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit &&\n\t\tcurQueueLength >= qs.qCfg.QueueLengthLimit {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\tqs.enqueueToBoundLocked(request)\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// enqueues a request into its queue.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit && qs.dispatchLocked() {\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (qs *queueSet) dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, This is so for a method that\n    82→// changes what request is oldest in a queue, because that change means\n    83→// that the anti-windup hack in boundNextDispatchLocked needs to be\n    84→// applied wrt the revised oldest request in the queue.\n    85→type queueSet struct {\n    86→\tclock                    eventclock.Interface\n    87→\testimatedServiceDuration time.Duration\n    88→\n    89→\treqsGaugePair metrics.RatioedGaugePair // .RequestsExecuting covers regular phase only\n    90→\n    91→\texecSeatsGauge metrics.RatioedGauge // for all phases of execution\n    92→\n    93→\tseatDemandIntegrator metrics.Gauge\n    94→\n    95→\tpromiseFactory promiseFactory\n    96→\n    97→\tlock sync.Mutex\n    98→\n    99→\t// qCfg holds the current queuing configuration.  254→func (qs *queueSet) setConfiguration(ctx context.Context, qCfg fq.QueuingConfig, dealer *shufflesharding.Dealer, dCfg fq.DispatchingConfig) {\n   255→\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\n   256→\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n   257→\n   258→\tif qCfg.DesiredNumQueues > 0 {\n   259→\t\t// Adding queues is the only thing that requires immediate action\n   260→\t\t// Removing queues is handled by attrition, 269→\t\tqCfg.HandSize = qs.qCfg.HandSize\n   270→\t}\n   271→\n   272→\tqs.qCfg = qCfg\n   273→\tqs.dCfg = dCfg\n   274→\tqs.dealer = dealer\n   275→\tqll := qCfg.QueueLengthLimit\n   276→\tif qll < 1 {\n   277→\t\tqll = 1\n   278→\t}\n   279→\tif qCfg.DesiredNumQueues > 0 {\n   280→\t\tqll *= qCfg.DesiredNumQueues\n   281→\t}\n 284→\tqs.execSeatsGauge.SetDenominator(float64(dCfg.ConcurrencyDenominator))\n   285→\n   286→\tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→// A decision about a request\n   290→type requestDecision int\n   291→\n   292→// Values passed through a request's decision\n   293→const (\n   294→\t// Serve this one\n   295→\tdecisionExecute requestDecision = iota\n   296→\n   297→\t// This one's context timed out / was canceled\n   298→\tdecisionCancel\n   299→)\n   300→\n   301→// StartRequest begins the process of handling a request.  We take the\n   302→// approach of updating the metrics about total requests queued and\n   303→// executing at each point where there is a change in that quantity,\n   304→// because the metrics --- and only the metrics --- track that\n   305→// quantity per FlowSchema.\n   306→// The queueSet's promiseFactory is invoked once if the returned Request is non-nil,\n   307→// not invoked if the Request is nil.\n   308→func (qs *queueSet) StartRequest(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) (fq.Request, bool) {\n   309→\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(ctx)\n   310→\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n   311→\tvar req *request\n   312→\n   313→\t// ========================================================================\n   314→\t// Step 0:\n   315→\t// Apply only concurrency limit, if zero queues desired\n   316→\tif qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 1 {\n   317→\t\tif !qs.canAccommodateSeatsLocked(workEstimate.MaxSeats()) {\n   318→\t\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v because %d seats are asked for, %d seats are in use (%d are executing) and the limit is %d\",\n   319→\t\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2, workEstimate, qs.totSeatsInUse, qs.totRequestsExecuting, qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)\n   320→\t\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n   321→\t\t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"concurrency-limit\")\n   322→\t\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n   323→\t\t}\n   324→\t\treq = qs.dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n   325→\t\treturn req, false\n   326→\t}\n   327→\n   328→\t// ========================================================================\n   329→\t// Step 1:\n   330→\t// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n   331→\t// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n   332→\t// we are at max queue length\n   333→\t// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n   334→\treq = qs.shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx, workEstimate, hashValue, flowDistinguisher, fsName, descr1, descr2, queueNoteFn)\n   335→\t// req == nil means that the request was rejected - no remaining\n   336→\t// concurrency shares and at max queue length already\n   337→\tif req == nil {\n   338→\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): rejecting request %q %#+v %#+v due to queue full\", qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, descr1, descr2)\n   339→\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n   340→\t\tmetrics.AddReject(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, \"queue-full\")\n   341→\t\treturn nil, qs.isIdleLocked()\n   342→\t}\n   343→\n   344→\t// ========================================================================\n   345→\t// Step 2:\n   346→\t// The next step is to invoke the method that dequeues as much\n   347→\t// as possible.\n   348→\t// This method runs a loop, as long as there are non-empty\n   349→\t// queues and the number currently executing is less than the\n   350→\t// assured concurrency value.  The body of the loop uses the\n   351→\t// fair queuing technique to pick a queue and dispatch a\n   352→\t// request from that queue.\n   353→\tqs.dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked()\n   354→\n   355→\treturn req, false\n   356→}\n   357→\n   358→// ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory is the promiseFactoryFactory that\n   359→// a queueSetFactory would ordinarily use.\n   360→// Test code might use something different.\n   361→func ordinaryPromiseFactoryFactory(qs *queueSet) promiseFactory {\n   362→\treturn promise.NewWriteOnce\n   363→}\n   364→\n   365→// MaxSeats returns the maximum number of seats this request requires, it is\n   366→// the maxumum of the two - WorkEstimate.InitialSeats, WorkEstimate.FinalSeats.\n   367→func (req *request) MaxSeats() int {\n   368→\treturn req.workEstimate.MaxSeats()\n   369→}\n   370→\n   371→func (req *request) InitialSeats() int {\n   372→\treturn int(req.workEstimate.InitialSeats)\n   373→}\n   374→\n   375→func (req *request) NoteQueued(inQueue bool) {\n   376→\tif req.queueNoteFn != nil {\n   377→\t\treq.queueNoteFn(inQueue)\n   378→\t}\n   379→}\n   380→\n   381→func (req *request) Finish(execFn func()) bool {\n   382→\texec, idle := req.wait()\n   383→\tif !exec {\n   384→\t\treturn idle\n   385→\t}\n   386→\tfunc() {\n   387→\t\tdefer func() {\n   388→\t\t\tidle = req.qs.finishRequestAndDispatchAsMuchAsPossible(req)\n   389→\t\t}()\n   390→\n   391→\t\texecFn()\n   392→\t}()\n   393→\n   394→\treturn idle\n   395→}\n   396→\n   397→func (req *request) wait() (bool, bool) {\n   398→\tqs := req.qs\n   399→\n   400→\t// ========================================================================\n   401→\t// Step 3:\n   402→\t// The final step is to wait on a decision from\n   403→\t// somewhere and then act on it.\n   404→\tdecisionAny := req.decision.Get()\n   405→\tqs.lockAndSyncTime(req.ctx)\n   406→\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n   407→\tif req.waitStarted {\n   408→\t\t// This can not happen, because the client is forbidden to\n   409→\t\t// call Wait twice on the same request\n   410→\t\tklog.Errorf(\"Duplicate call to the Wait method!  Immediately returning execute=false.  QueueSet=%s, startTime=%s, descr1=%#+v, descr2=%#+v\", req.qs.qCfg.Name, req.startTime, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n   411→\t\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n   412→\t}\n   413→\treq.waitStarted = true\n   414→\tswitch decisionAny {\n   415→\tcase decisionCancel: // handle in code following this switch\n   416→\tcase decisionExecute:\n   417→\t\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Dispatching request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n   418→\t\treturn true, false\n   419→\tdefault:\n   420→\t\t// This can not happen, all possible values are handled above\n   421→\t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s): Impossible decision (type %T, value %#+v) for request %#+v %#+v!  Treating as cancel\", qs.qCfg.Name, decisionAny, decisionAny, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n   422→\t}\n   423→\t// TODO(aaron-prindle) add metrics for this case\n   424→\tklog.V(5).Infof(\"QS(%s): Ejecting request %#+v %#+v from its queue\", qs.qCfg.Name, req.descr1, req.descr2)\n   425→\t// remove the request from the queue as its queue wait time has exceeded\n   426→\tqueue := req.queue\n   427→\tif req.removeFromQueueLocked() != nil {\n   428→\t\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n   429→\t\tqs.totRequestsWaiting--\n   430→\t\tqs.totSeatsWaiting -= req.MaxSeats()\n   431→\t\tqs.totRequestsRejected++\n   432→\t\tqs.totRequestsCancelled++\n   433→\t\tmetrics.AddReject(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, \"time-out\")\n   434→\t\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -1)\n   435→\t\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(req.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, req.fsName, -req.MaxSeats())\n   436→\t\treq.NoteQueued(false)\n   437→\t\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(-1)\n   438→\t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   439→\t}\n   440→\treturn false, qs.isIdleLocked()\n   441→}\n   442→\n   443→func (qs *queueSet) IsIdle() bool {\n   444→\tqs.lock.Lock()\n   445→\tdefer qs.lock.Unlock()\n   446→\treturn qs.isIdleLocked()\n   447→}\n   448→\n   449→func (qs *queueSet) isIdleLocked() bool {\n   450→\treturn qs.totRequestsWaiting == 0 && qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0\n   451→}\n   452→\n   453→// lockAndSyncTime acquires the lock and updates the virtual time.\n   454→// Doing them together avoids the mistake of modifying some queue state\n   455→// before calling syncTimeLocked.\n   456→func (qs *queueSet) lockAndSyncTime(ctx context.Context) {\n   457→\tqs.lock.Lock()\n   458→\tqs.syncTimeLocked(ctx)\n   459→}\n   460→\n   461→// syncTimeLocked updates the virtual time based on the assumption\n   462→// that the current state of the queues has been in effect since\n   463→// `qs.lastRealTime`.  Thus, it should be invoked after acquiring the\n   464→// lock and before modifying the state of any queue.\n   465→func (qs *queueSet) syncTimeLocked(ctx context.Context) {\n   466→\trealNow := qs.clock.Now()\n   467→\ttimeSinceLast := realNow.Sub(qs.lastRealTime)\n   468→\tqs.lastRealTime = realNow\n   469→\tprevR := qs.currentR\n   470→\tincrR := fqrequest.SeatsTimesDuration(qs.getVirtualTimeRatioLocked(), timeSinceLast)\n   471→\tqs.currentR = prevR + incrR\n   472→\tswitch {\n   473→\tcase prevR > qs.currentR:\n   474→\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queueset::currentR overflow\"), \"Overflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", realNow.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"prevR\", prevR, \"incrR\", incrR, \"currentR\", qs.currentR)\n   475→\tcase qs.currentR >= highR:\n   476→\t\tqs.advanceEpoch(ctx, realNow, incrR)\n   477→\t}\n   478→\tmetrics.SetCurrentR(qs.qCfg.Name, qs.currentR.ToFloat())\n   479→}\n   480→\n   481→// rDecrement is the amount by which the progress meter R is wound backwards\n   482→// when needed to avoid overflow.\n   483→const rDecrement = fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds / 2\n   484→\n   485→// highR is the threshold that triggers advance of the epoch.\n   486→// That is, decrementing the global progress meter R by rDecrement.\n   487→const highR = rDecrement + rDecrement/2\n   488→\n   489→// advanceEpoch subtracts rDecrement from the global progress meter R\n   490→// and all the readings that have been taked from that meter.\n   491→// The now and incrR parameters are only used to add info to the log messages.\n   492→func (qs *queueSet) advanceEpoch(ctx context.Context, now time.Time, incrR fqrequest.SeatSeconds) {\n   493→\toldR := qs.currentR\n   494→\tqs.currentR -= rDecrement\n   495→\tklog.InfoS(\"Advancing epoch\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"when\", now.Format(nsTimeFmt), \"oldR\", oldR, \"newR\", qs.currentR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n   496→\tsuccess := true\n   497→\tfor qIdx, queue := range qs.queues {\n   498→\t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 {\n   499→\t\t\t// Do not just decrement, the value could be quite outdated.\n   500→\t\t\t// It is safe to reset to zero in this case, because the next request\n   501→\t\t\t// will overwrite the zero with `qs.currentR`.\n   502→\t\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = 0\n   503→\t\t\tcontinue\n   504→\t\t}\n   505→\t\toldNextDispatchR := queue.nextDispatchR\n   506→\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR -= rDecrement\n   507→\t\tif queue.nextDispatchR > oldNextDispatchR {\n   508→\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"queue::nextDispatchR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"oldNextDispatchR\", oldNextDispatchR, \"newNextDispatchR\", queue.nextDispatchR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n   509→\t\t\tsuccess = false\n   510→\t\t}\n   511→\t\tqueue.requestsWaiting.Walk(func(req *request) bool {\n   512→\t\t\toldArrivalR := req.arrivalR\n   513→\t\t\treq.arrivalR -= rDecrement\n   514→\t\t\tif req.arrivalR > oldArrivalR {\n   515→\t\t\t\tklog.ErrorS(errors.New(\"request::arrivalR underflow\"), \"Underflow\", \"QS\", qs.qCfg.Name, \"queue\", qIdx, \"request\", *req, \"oldArrivalR\", oldArrivalR, \"incrR\", incrR)\n   516→\t\t\t\tsuccess = false\n   517→\t\t\t}\n   518→\t\t\treturn true\n   519→\t\t})\n   520→\t}\n   521→\tmetrics.AddEpochAdvance(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, success)\n   522→}\n   523→\n   524→// getVirtualTimeRatio calculates the rate at which virtual time has\n   525→// been advancing, according to the logic in `doc.go`.\n   526→func (qs *queueSet) getVirtualTimeRatioLocked() float64 {\n   527→\tactiveQueues := 0\n   528→\tseatsRequested := 0\n   529→\tfor _, queue := range qs.queues {\n   530→\t\t// here we want the sum of the maximum width of the requests in this queue since our\n   531→\t\t// goal is to find the maximum rate at which the queue could work.\n   532→\t\tseatsRequested += (queue.seatsInUse + queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum().MaxSeatsSum)\n   533→\t\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() > 0 || queue.requestsExecuting.Len() > 0 {\n   534→\t\t\tactiveQueues++\n   535→\t\t}\n   536→\t}\n   537→\tif activeQueues == 0 {\n   538→\t\treturn 0\n   539→\t}\n   540→\treturn math.Min(float64(seatsRequested), float64(qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit)) / float64(activeQueues)\n   541→}\n   542→\n   543→// shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked encapsulates the logic required\n   544→// to validate and enqueue a request for the queueSet/QueueSet:\n   545→// 1) Start with shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n   546→// 2) Reject current request if there is not enough concurrency shares and\n   547→// we are at max queue length\n   548→// 3) If not rejected, create a request and enqueue\n   549→// returns the enqueud request on a successful enqueue\n   550→// returns nil in the case that there is no available concurrency or\n   551→// the queuelengthlimit has been reached\n   552→func (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardAndRejectOrEnqueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, hashValue uint64, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}, queueNoteFn fq.QueueNoteFn) *request {\n   553→\t// Start with the shuffle sharding, to pick a queue.\n   554→\tqueueIdx := qs.shuffleShardLocked(hashValue, descr1, descr2)\n   555→\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n   556→\n   557→\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n   558→\n   559→\t// Create a request and enqueue\n   560→\treq := &request{\n   561→\t\tqs:                qs,\n   562→\t\tfsName:            fsName,\n   563→\t\tflowDistinguisher: flowDistinguisher,\n   564→\t\tctx:               ctx,\n   565→\t\tdecision:          qs.promiseFactory(nil, ctx, decisionCancel),\n   566→\t\tarrivalTime:       qs.clock.Now(),\n   567→\t\tarrivalR:          qs.currentR,\n   568→\t\tqueue:             queue,\n   569→\t\tdescr1:            descr1,\n   570→\t\tdescr2:            descr2,\n   571→\t\tqueueNoteFn:       queueNoteFn,\n   572→\t\tworkEstimate:      qs.completeWorkEstimate(workEstimate),\n   573→\t}\n   574→\tif ok := qs.rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(req); !ok {\n   575→\t\treturn nil\n   576→\t}\n   577→\tmetrics.ObserveQueueLength(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, queue.requestsWaiting.Length())\n   578→\treturn req\n   579→}\n   580→\n   581→// shuffleShardLocked uses shuffle sharding to select a queue index\n   582→// using the given hashValue and the shuffle sharding parameters of the queueSet.\n   583→func (qs *queueSet) shuffleShardLocked(hashValue uint64, descr1, descr2 interface{}) int {\n   584→\tvar backHand [8]int\n   585→\t// Deal into a data structure, so that the order of visit below is not necessarily the order of the deal.\n   586→\t// This removes bias in the case of flows with overlapping hands.\n   587→\thand := qs.dealer.DealIntoHand(hashValue, backHand[:])\n   588→\thandSize := len(hand)\n   589→\toffset := qs.enqueues % handSize\n   590→\tqs.enqueues++\n   591→\tbestQueueIdx := -1\n   592→\tminQueueSeatSeconds := fqrequest.MaxSeatSeconds\n   593→\tfor i := 0; i < handSize; i++ {\n   594→\t\tqueueIdx := hand[(offset+i)%handSize]\n   595→\t\tqueue := qs.queues[queueIdx]\n   596→\t\tqueueSum := queue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum()\n   597→\n   598→\t\t// this is the total amount of work in seat-seconds for requests\n   599→\t\t// waiting in this queue, we will select the queue with the minimum.\n   600→\t\tthisQueueSeatSeconds := queueSum.TotalWorkSum\n   601→\t\tklog.V(7).Infof(\"QS(%s): For request %#+v %#+v considering queue %d with sum: %#v and %d seats in use, nextDispatchR=%v\", qs.qCfg.Name, descr1, descr2, queueIdx, queueSum, queue.seatsInUse, queue.nextDispatchR)\n   602→\t\tif thisQueueSeatSeconds < minQueueSeatSeconds {\n   603→\t\t\tminQueueSeatSeconds = thisQueueSeatSeconds\n   604→\t\t\tbestQueueIdx = queueIdx\n   605→\t\t}\n   606→\t}\n   607→\tif klogV := klog.V(6); klogV.Enabled() {\n   608→\t\tchosenQueue := qs.queues[bestQueueIdx]\n   609→\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: For request %#+v %#+v chose queue %d, with sum: %#v & %d seats in use & nextDispatchR=%v\", qs.qCfg.Name, qs.clock.Now().Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, descr1, descr2, bestQueueIdx, chosenQueue.requestsWaiting.QueueSum(), chosenQueue.seatsInUse, chosenQueue.nextDispatchR)\n   610→\t}\n   611→\treturn bestQueueIdx\n   612→}\n   613→\n   614→// rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked rejects or enqueues the newly arrived\n   615→// request, which has been assigned to a queue.  If up against the\n   616→// queue length limit and the concurrency limit then returns false.\n   617→// Otherwise enqueues and returns true.\n   618→func (qs *queueSet) rejectOrEnqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) bool {\n   619→\tqueue := request.queue\n   620→\tcurQueueLength := queue.requestsWaiting.Length()\n   621→\t// rejects the newly arrived request if resource criteria not met\n   622→\tif qs.totSeatsInUse >= qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit &&\n   623→\t\tcurQueueLength >= qs.qCfg.QueueLengthLimit {\n   624→\t\treturn false\n   625→\t}\n   626→\n   627→\tqs.enqueueToBoundLocked(request)\n   628→\treturn true\n   629→}\n   630→\n   631→// enqueues a request into its queue.\n   632→func (qs *queueSet) enqueueToBoundLocked(request *request) {\n   633→\tqueue := request.queue\n   634→\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n   635→\tif queue.requestsWaiting.Length() == 0 && queue.requestsExecuting.Len() == 0 {\n   636→\t\t// the queue’s start R is set to the virtual time.\n   637→\t\tqueue.nextDispatchR = qs.currentR\n   638→\t\tklogV := klog.V(6)\n   639→\t\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n   640→\t\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: initialized queue %d start R due to request %#+v %#+v\", qs.qCfg.Name, now.Format(nsTimeFmt), queue.nextDispatchR, queue.index, request.descr1, request.descr2)\n   641→\t\t}\n   642→\t}\n   643→\trequest.removeFromQueueLocked = queue.requestsWaiting.Enqueue(request)\n   644→\tqs.totRequestsWaiting++\n   645→\tqs.totSeatsWaiting += request.MaxSeats()\n   646→\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, 1)\n   647→\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, request.MaxSeats())\n   648→\trequest.NoteQueued(true)\n   649→\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(1)\n   650→\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   651→}\n   652→\n   653→// dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked does as many dispatches as possible now.\n   654→func (qs *queueSet) dispatchAsMuchAsPossibleLocked() {\n   655→\tfor qs.totRequestsWaiting != 0 && qs.totSeatsInUse < qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit && qs.dispatchLocked() {\n   656→\t}\n   657→}\n   658→\n   659→func (qs *queueSet) dispatchSansQueueLocked(ctx context.Context, workEstimate *fqrequest.WorkEstimate, flowDistinguisher, fsName string, descr1, descr2 interface{}) *request {\n   660→\t// does not call metrics.SetDispatchMetrics because there is no queuing and thus no interesting virtual world\n   661→\tnow := qs.clock.Now()\n   662→\treq := &request{\n   663→\t\tqs:                qs,\n   664→\t\tfsName:            fsName,\n   665→\t\tflowDistinguisher: flowDistinguisher,\n   666→\t\tctx:               ctx,\n   667→\t\tstartTime:         now,\n   668→\t\tdecision:          qs.promiseFactory(decisionExecute, ctx, decisionCancel),\n   669→\t\tarrivalTime:       now,\n   670→\t\tarrivalR:          qs.currentR,\n   671→\t\tdescr1:            descr1,\n   672→\t\tdescr2:            descr2,\n   673→\t\tworkEstimate:      qs.completeWorkEstimate(workEstimate),\n   674→\t}\n   675→\tqs.totRequestsExecuting++\n   676→\tqs.totSeatsInUse += req.MaxSeats()\n   677→\tqs.requestsExecutingSet = qs.requestsExecutingSet.Insert(req)\n   678→\tmetrics.AddRequestsExecuting(ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, 1)\n   679→\tmetrics.AddSeatConcurrencyInUse(qs.qCfg.Name, fsName, req.MaxSeats())\n   680→\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.Add(1)\n   681→\tqs.execSeatsGauge.Add(float64(req.MaxSeats()))\n   682→\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   683→\tklogV := klog.V(5)\n   684→\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n   685→\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: immediate dispatch of request %q %#+v %#+v, qs will have %d executing\", qs.qCfg.Name, now.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, fsName, descr1, descr2, qs.totRequestsExecuting)\n   686→\t}\n   687→\treturn req\n   688→}\n   689→\n   690→// dispatchLocked uses the Fair Queuing for Server Requests method to\n   691→// select a queue and dispatch the oldest request in that queue.  The\n   692→// return value indicates whether a request was dequeued; this will\n   693→// be false when either all queues are empty or the request at the head\n   694→// of the next queue cannot be dispatched.\n   695→func (qs *queueSet) dispatchLocked() bool {\n   696→\tqueue, request := qs.findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked()\n   697→\tif queue == nil {\n   698→\t\treturn false\n   699→\t}\n   700→\tif request == nil { // This should never happen.  But if it does...\n   701→\t\treturn false\n   702→\t}\n   703→\tqs.totRequestsWaiting--\n   704→\tqs.totSeatsWaiting -= request.MaxSeats()\n   705→\tmetrics.AddRequestsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, -1)\n   706→\tmetrics.AddSeatsInQueues(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, -request.MaxSeats())\n   707→\trequest.NoteQueued(false)\n   708→\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsWaiting.Add(-1)\n   709→\tdefer qs.boundNextDispatchLocked(queue)\n   710→\tif !request.decision.Set(decisionExecute) {\n   711→\t\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   712→\t\treturn true\n   713→\t}\n   714→\trequest.startTime = qs.clock.Now()\n   715→\t// At this moment the request leaves its queue and starts\n   716→\t// executing.  We do not recognize any interim state between\n   717→\t// \"queued\" and \"executing\".  While that means \"executing\"\n   718→\t// includes a little overhead from this package, this is not a\n   719→\t// problem because other overhead is also included.\n   720→\tqs.totRequestsExecuting++\n   721→\tqs.totSeatsInUse += request.MaxSeats()\n   722→\tqueue.requestsExecuting = queue.requestsExecuting.Insert(request)\n   723→\tqueue.seatsInUse += request.MaxSeats()\n   724→\tmetrics.AddRequestsExecuting(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, 1)\n   725→\tmetrics.AddSeatConcurrencyInUse(qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, request.MaxSeats())\n   726→\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.Add(1)\n   727→\tqs.execSeatsGauge.Add(float64(request.MaxSeats()))\n   728→\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n   729→\tklogV := klog.V(6)\n   730→\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n   731→\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: dispatching request %#+v %#+v work %v from queue %d with start R %v, queue will have %d waiting & %d requests occupying %d seats, set will have %d seats occupied\",\n   732→\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, request.startTime.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, request.descr1, request.descr2,\n   733→\t\t\trequest.workEstimate, queue.index, queue.nextDispatchR, queue.requestsWaiting.Length(), queue.requestsExecuting.Len(), queue.seatsInUse, qs.totSeatsInUse)\n   734→\t}\n   735→\t// When a request is dequeued for service -> qs.virtualStart += G * width\n   736→\tif request.totalWork() > rDecrement/100 { // A single increment should never be so big\n   737→\t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: dispatching request %#+v %#+v with implausibly high work %v from queue %d with start R %v\",\n   738→\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, request.startTime.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, request.descr1, request.descr2,\n   739→\t\t\trequest.workEstimate, queue.index, queue.nextDispatchR)\n   740→\t}\n   741→\tqueue.nextDispatchR += request.totalWork()\n   742→\treturn true\n   743→}\n   744→\n   745→// canAccommodateSeatsLocked returns true if this queueSet has enough\n   746→// seats available to accommodate a request with the given number of seats,\n   747→// otherwise it returns false.\n   748→func (qs *queueSet) canAccommodateSeatsLocked(seats int) bool {\n   749→\tswitch {\n   750→\tcase qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 0:\n   751→\t\t// This is code for exemption from limitation\n   752→\t\treturn true\n   753→\tcase seats > qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit:\n   754→\t\t// we have picked the queue with the minimum virtual finish time, but\n   755→\t\t// the number of seats this request asks for exceeds the concurrency limit.\n   756→\t\t// TODO: this is a quick fix for now, once we have borrowing in place we will not need it\n   757→\t\tif qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0 {\n   758→\t\t\t// TODO: apply additional lateny associated with this request, as described in the KEP\n   759→\t\t\treturn true\n   760→\t\t}\n   761→\t\t// wait for all \"currently\" executing requests in this queueSet\n   762→\t\t// to finish before we can execute this request.\n   763→\t\treturn false\n   764→\tcase qs.totSeatsInUse+seats > qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit:\n   765→\t\treturn false\n queueset\n\nimport (\n\t\"container/list\"\n)\n\n// removeFromFIFOFunc removes a designated element from the list\n// if that element is in the list.\n// The complexity of the runtime cost is O(1).\n// The returned value is the element removed, if indeed one was removed,\n// otherwise `nil`.\ntype removeFromFIFOFunc func() *request\n\n// walkFunc is called for each request in the list in the\n// oldest -> newest order.\n// ok: if walkFunc returns false then the iteration stops immediately.\n// walkFunc may remove the given request from the fifo,\n// but may not mutate the fifo in any othe way.\ntype walkFunc func(*request) (ok bool)\n\n// Internal interface to abstract out the implementation details\n// of the underlying list used to maintain the requests.\n//\n// Note that a fifo, including the removeFromFIFOFuncs returned from Enqueue,\n// is not safe for concurrent use by multiple goroutines.\ntype fifo interface {\n\t// Enqueue enqueues the specified request into the list and\n\t// returns a removeFromFIFOFunc function that can be used to remove the\n\t// request from the list\n\tEnqueue(*request) removeFromFIFOFunc\n\n\t// Dequeue pulls out the oldest request from the list.\n\tDequeue() (*request, bool)\n\n\t// Peek returns the oldest request without removing it.\n\tPeek() (*request, bool)\n\n\t// Length returns the number of requests in the list.\n\tLength() int\n\n\t// QueueSum returns the sum of initial seats, final seats, and\n\t// additional latency aggregated from all requests in this queue.\n\tQueueSum() queueSum\n\n\t// Walk iterates through the list in order of oldest -> newest\n\t// and executes the specified walkFunc for each request in that order.\n\t//\n\t// if the specified walkFunc returns false the Walk function\n\t// stops the walk an returns immediately.\n\tWalk(walkFunc)\n}\n\n// the FIFO list implementation is not safe for concurrent use by multiple\n// goroutines.\ntype requestFIFO struct {\n\t*list.List\n\n\tsum queueSum\n}\n\nfunc newRequestFIFO() fifo {\n\treturn &requestFIFO{\n\t\tList: list.New(),\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (l *requestFIFO) Length() int {\n\treturn l.Len()\n}\n\nfunc (l *request {\n\t\tif e.Value == nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\tl.Remove(e)\n\t\te.Value = nil\n\t\tdeductFromQueueSum(&l.sum, req)\n\t\treturn req\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (l *requestFIFO) Dequeue() (*request, bool) {\n\treturn l.getFirst(true)\n}\n\nfunc (l *requestFIFO) Peek() (*request, bool) {\n\treturn l.getFirst(false)\n}\n\nfunc (l *requestFIFO) getFirst(remove bool) (*request, bool) += request.MaxSeats()\n\tqueue.requestsExecuting = queue.requestsExecuting.Insert(request)\n\tqueue.seatsInUse += request.MaxSeats()\n\tmetrics.AddRequestsExecuting(request.ctx, qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, 1)\n\tmetrics.AddSeatConcurrencyInUse(qs.qCfg.Name, request.fsName, request.MaxSeats())\n\tqs.reqsGaugePair.RequestsExecuting.Add(1)\n\tqs.execSeatsGauge.Add(float64(request.MaxSeats()))\n\tqs.seatDemandIntegrator.Set(float64(qs.totSeatsInUse + qs.totSeatsWaiting))\n\tklogV := klog.V(6)\n\tif klogV.Enabled() {\n\t\tklogV.Infof(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: dispatching request %#+v %#+v work %v from queue %d with start R %v, queue will have %d waiting & %d requests occupying %d seats, set will have %d seats occupied\",\n\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, request.startTime.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, request.descr1, request.descr2,\n\t\t\trequest.workEstimate, queue.index, queue.nextDispatchR, queue.requestsWaiting.Length(), queue.requestsExecuting.Len(), queue.seatsInUse, qs.totSeatsInUse)\n\t}\n\t// When a request is dequeued for service -> qs.virtualStart += G * width\n\tif request.totalWork() > rDecrement/100 { // A single increment should never be so big\n\t\tklog.Errorf(\"QS(%s) at t=%s R=%v: dispatching request %#+v %#+v with implausibly high work %v from queue %d with start R %v\",\n\t\t\tqs.qCfg.Name, request.startTime.Format(nsTimeFmt), qs.currentR, request.descr1, request.descr2,\n\t\t\trequest.workEstimate, queue.index, queue.nextDispatchR)\n\t}\n\tqueue.nextDispatchR += request.totalWork()\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// canAccommodateSeatsLocked returns true if this queueSet has enough\n// seats available to accommodate a request with the given number of seats,\n// otherwise it returns false.\nfunc (qs *queueSet) canAccommodateSeatsLocked(seats int) bool {\n\tswitch {\n\tcase qs.qCfg.DesiredNumQueues < 0:\n\t\t// This is code for exemption from limitation\n\t\treturn true\n\tcase seats > qs.dCfg.ConcurrencyLimit:\n\t\t// we have picked the queue with the minimum virtual finish time, but\n\t\t// the number of seats this request asks for exceeds the concurrency limit.\n\t\t// TODO: this is a quick fix for now, once we have borrowing in place we will not need it\n\t\tif qs.totRequestsExecuting == 0 {\n\t\t\t// TODO: apply additional lateny associated with this request, as described in the KEP\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t\t// wait for all false\n\t}\n\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// findDispatchQueueToBoundLocked examines the queues in round robin order and\n// returns the first one of those for which the virtual finish time of\n// the oldest qs.estimatedServiceDuration)\n\t\t\tdsMin = min(dsMin, queue.nextDispatchR-estimatedWorkInProgress)\n\t\t\tdsMax = max(dsMax, queue.nextDispatchR-estimatedWorkInProgress)\n\t\t\tcurrentVirtualFinish given demands (which slice is not side-effected).\n    52→func fairAlloc(demands []float64, capacity float64) []float64 {\n    53→\tcount := len(demands)\n    54→\tindices := make([]int, count)\n    55→\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n    56→\t\tindices[i] = i\n    57→\t}\n    58→\tsort.Slice(indices, func(i, j int) bool { return demands[indices[i]] < demands[indices[j]] })\n    59→\talloc := make([]float64, count)\n    60→\tvar next int\n    61→\tvar prevAlloc float64\n    62→\tfor ; next < count; next++ {\n    63→\t\t// `capacity` is how much remains assuming that\n    64→\t\t// all unvisited items get `prevAlloc`.\n    65→\t\tidx := indices[next]\n    66→\t\tdemand := demands[idx]\n    67→\t\tif demand <= 0 {\n    68→\t\t\tcontinue\n    69→\t\t}\n    70→\t\t// `fullCapacityBite` is how much more capacity would be used\n    71→\t\t// if this and all following items get as much as this one\n    72→\t\t// is demanding.\n    73→\t\tfullCapacityBite := float64(count-next) * (demand - prevAlloc)\n    74→\t\tif fullCapacityBite > capacity {\n    75→\t\t\tbreak\n    76→\t\t}\n    77→\t\tprevAlloc = demand\n    78→\t\talloc[idx] = demand\n    79→\t\tcapacity -= fullCapacityBite\n    80→\t}\n    81→\tfor j := next; j < count; j++ {\n    82→\t\talloc[indices[j]] = prevAlloc + capacity/float64(count-next)\n    83→\t}\n    84→\treturn alloc\n    85→}\n    86→\n side-effected).\nfunc fairAlloc(demands []float64, capacity float64) []float64 {\n\tcount := len(demands)\n\tindices := make([]int, count)\n\tfor i := 0; i < count; i++ {\n\t\tindices[i] = i\n\t}\n\tsort.Slice(indices, func(i, j int) bool { return demands[indices[i]] < demands[indices[j]] })\n\talloc := make([]float64, count)\n\tvar next int\n\tvar prevAlloc float64\n\tfor ; next < count; next++ {\n\t\t// `capacity` is how much remains assuming that\n\t\t// all unvisited items get `prevAlloc`.\n\t\tidx := indices[next]\n\t\tdemand := demands[idx]\n\t\tif demand <= 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t\t// `fullCapacityBite` is how much more capacity would be used\n\t\t// if this and all following items get as much as this one\n\t\t// is demanding.\n\t\tfullCapacityBite := float64(count-next) * (demand - prevAlloc)\n\t\tif fullCapacityBite > capacity {\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t\tprevAlloc = demand\n\t\talloc[idx] = demand\n\t\tcapacity -= fullCapacityBite\n\t}\n\tfor j := next; j < count; j++ {\n\t\talloc[indices[j]] = prevAlloc + capacity/float64(count-next)\n\t}\n\treturn alloc\n}\n\nfunc TestFairAlloc(t *testing.T) {\n\tif e, a := []float64{0, 0},
